<Review>I recently rented a space at the 1909 Old Middlefield Public Storage for 1.5 months. I highly recommend this location. I really got I paid for -- everything about the operation felt thought out and professional.

The access gates work perfectly; you get your car in and out of the lot without worrying about getting sandwiched! The large carts make it easy to transport many items at once. The elevators pause for a minute on opening and closing to give you plenty of time to wheel your cart in and out. And every time I was there, the outside and inside of the facility was tidy. I remember once hearing a brief brushing sound down my hall and it was James, the manager, on one of his walkthroughs, doing a quick sweep.

Another great thing about this location is the trees hanging over the parking spots. My car stayed cool.

More about James -- on first meeting, without me asking he described the safety of the facility (no transactions permitted on site; local police expect the facility to be quiet and it gets their attention when it isn‚Äôt).

Not only is James on top of everything, he is warm and funny.

One tip. If you are storing clothes you want to hang, you can buy a "wardrobe box" at the office and it is well worth spending a couple of extra bucks to get the large size one. It was a big help.</Review><date>1464747153623</date>< user>

Awesome French restaurant. Their menu is just great, lots of variety. Their onion soup is super tasty, so are the mussels with fries. Their wine menu is great, they have Chablis. < Review>
Overall I can strongly recommend Citadel.  They were by far the best price I got (and I met with several local solar companies as you should before signing a contract).  We went into contract in early May 2020.  COVID presented a few challenges for us, and probably was the main cause of us not getting an install until late July.  However, the install was almost flawless with a truly professional crew.  Simply cannot praise them enough.  They did an amazing job with hiding the conduit so it was entirely invisible.  The panels are low rise (see photo) and while I expected the panels to be more imposing you really don't know they are there.  Also, as a roofing company, they understood how to deal with a cement tile roof installation.

We went with their recommended panels (REC) 320 watt even though most installers are selling 350 watt panels now.  320 watt are sort of "last year's model" but we had room for additional panels and going with the 320 watt panels saved money.  If you are getting high quotes for 350 watt panel installation this is a possible alternative for you.

I will say I considered holding back one star because of the project management process.  Our sales contact Gideon was terrific, but the handoff to project management had a few bumps.  It seems like their project managers are stretched thin, and as a result we did not get the attention we should have during the long wait between contract execution and installation. While that was frustrating at times it was not a dealbreaker. In the end our project manager rebounded and managed the permit process and installation coordination well so he earned back that last star.  He was easy to work with but would have benefited from a little more supervision? As I said not a dealbreaker just an area for improvement for Citadel to take note.

Our first bill post-solar full month bill is is due in September but the system has been cranking since day one.  You can feel comfortable going with Citadel for this investment!  We are very pleased with this job.

PROS:  Very competitive price; very professional company with excellent installation; good customer support (so far); smooth installation process with highly qualified installers; honest; fair

CONS: Some lag time after contract execution; project support lagged at times prior to installation.

PROJECT: 23 solar panels with a main panel upgrade.  7.36kW system.  Enphase IQ7 inverters. REC320NP solar panels.

COST: $23,000 +/- including main panel upgrade.

EXPECTED TAX CREDIT: $6,000.  Net cost $17,000 +/-.</Review>

<user_name>Natalie Groce<//user_name><date>1603558332884< /date><Rating>5</Rating>< review>
We foster-failed two sweet dogs in June and one of them has chronic ear issues. Dr. Michelle and the whole team at Petsadena have been wonderful. Rather than just treating the ear infections with antibiotics Dr. Michelle helped figure out the root cause - food allergies. Every single person on the staff that I've interacted with has been a delight and I feel safe leaving our sweet fur babies in their care. The Covid procedures are excellent - video chats during appointments as well as all of the techs wearing masks and face shields. It's not inexpensive but the cost of care is always given up front before anything is done. They're also extremely helpful when I call with what feels like a "dumb question" taking the time to look at our dog's chart and offering advice. I would absolutely reccomend Petsadena to any friend looking for a vet.</review>

<Text>Yippee Dog Yeah!!!!
Me and my Charles Theodore Barkley are so happy and grateful to have Dr. Evelyn as his doctor.

He had surgery for a torn ACL and a floating Patella. They did is surgery (11yrs. old.) She came early to reassure. He was there for 6 weeks getting, laser and PT.

He looks better than before. The cost was 1/2 of what others quoted. She also helped me find funding from various charity. I'm on SSI.

I know so many of us we concerned about the great care of our pet families after Dr. K  came after his severe auto car accident. He and his daughter were the best I've ever met.

Dr. E provides the same level of care, as they did and perhaps a little more. I drive 1 hr to see them. It's always worth the drive. Plus, she remembers everybody's name. Stunning!. Makes me feel like they care!

As far of the turn over, I've spoken to a few, asked them why they were leaving.

The responses, they wanted to go back to school to study vet science.

Many are young still trying to decide what they want aa acareer. One woman moved back home out of state.

A few wanted to find somewhere closer work. I recognize her drive time. Its as long as mine.One wanted to learn how to be a groomer instead.

Enough said !!!! No body made us stay, somebody over there must be doing something right .

Thanks Petsadena

<time>1569398707967< /time><text>This is a nice little park in West Covina. My boys played Little League here but sadly the league folded due to a lack of volunteers. This is why the baseball fields are not kept up.
There are lighted tennis courts that get quite a bit of use.
There are also basketball courts which are very busy most of the time.
There is a large community center that is used by various organizations for classes and other activities. The center has a kitchen as well as tables and chairs and can be rented for private parties. Just contact the city of West Covina if interested. A lot of beautiful views from the top of this park as it is elevated which means that it gets cool there in the evening times.  A lot of parking as well. I have spent alot of time in this park with my wife and children creating thousands of great memories. I am sure if you take your family there you will create some nice memories as well!< /text></record>
